clip: rect(3.427em 1000.42em 4.371em -999.997em); top: -4.011em; left: 0em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1522" style="font-family: STIXGeneral; font-style: italic;">y</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.017em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -4.365em; left: 0.475em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1523" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: STIXGeneral;">2</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.017em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1524" style="font-family: STIXGeneral;">)</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.017em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.903em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1525" style="vertical-align: 2.246em;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.475em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; font-family: STIXSizeOneSym; top: -3.303em; left: 0em;">⎤<span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.017em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; font-family: STIXSizeOneSym; top: -0.292em; left: 0em;">⎦<span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.017em;"></span></span><span style="font-family: STIXSizeOneSym; position: absolute; top: -2.594em; left: 0em;">⎥<span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.017em;"></span></span><span style="font-family: STIXSizeOneSym; position: absolute; top: -1.827em; left: 0em;">⎥<span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.017em;"></span></span><span style="font-family: STIXSizeOneSym; position: absolute; top: -1.06em; left: 0em;">⎥<span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.017em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.607em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -2.211em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 5.004em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML MJX_Assistive_MathML_Block" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><mi>R</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">q</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>[</mo><mtable rowspacing="4pt" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>+</mo><msup><mi>z</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mtd><mtd><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mi>y</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>z</mi><mi>w</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mtd><mtd><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mi>z</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>y</mi><mi>w</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mi>y</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>z</mi><mi>w</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mtd><mtd><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>x</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>+</mo><msup><mi>z</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mtd><mtd><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>y</mi><mi>z</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>x</mi><mi>w</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mi>z</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>y</mi><mi>w</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mtd><mtd><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>y</mi><mi>z</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>x</mi><mi>w</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mtd><mtd><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>x</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>+</mo><msup><mi>y</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mtd></mtr></mtable><mo>]</mo></mrow></math></span></span></div><script type="math/tex; mode=display" id="MathJax-Element-36"> R(\mathbf{q}) =         \begin{bmatrix}         1-2(y^2 + z^2) & 2(xy - zw) & 2(xz + yw) \\         2(xy + zw) & 1-2(x^2 + z^2) & 2(yz - xw) \\         2(xz - yw) & 2(yz + xw) & 1-2(x^2 + y^2)         \end{bmatrix} </script></p>
<p>这里的推导用到了轴-角旋转表示中的<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rodrigues%27_rotation_formula" target="_blank" rel="external">Rodrigues’ rotation formula</a>，具体证明这里不展开了，有兴趣的可以查阅相关资料。</p>
<p>我们发现用四元数描述旋转需要的存储空间很小，更为关键的是可以使用被称为<em>球面线性插值</em>（<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slerp" target="_blank" rel="external">Slerp Algorithm</a>）的方法对四元数进行插值运算，从而解决了平滑旋转的插值问题。</p>
<p>在 OpenGL 或者 DirectX 中我们通常使用模型视图矩阵来进行几何变换，当我们希望实现光滑旋转、对旋转进行插值时，就可以利用四元数这一工具。处理过程为：</p>
<ul>
<li>模型视图矩阵 -&gt; 四元数</li>
<li>使用四元数进行运算</li>
<li>四元数 -&gt; 模型视图矩阵</li>
</ul>

      
    </div>
